Aŋguttara Nikāya
Catukka Nipāta
XXVIII: Rāgādi-Peyyālaɱ

Sutta 271
or [271-287] or [271-780]

Rāgādi-Peyyālaɱ

Adapted from the 1995 edition of the digital version of the Sri Lanka Buddha Jayanti Tripitaka Series.

 

[Rāgassa] [Dosassa] [Mohassa] [Kodhassa] [Upanāhassa] [Makkhassa] [Paḷāsassa] [Issāya] [Macchariyassa] [Māyāya] [Sāṭheyyassa] [Thambhassa] [Sārambhassa] [Mānassa] [Atimānassa] [Madassa] [Pamādassa]

 

[256]

[1][pts][bodh] Evaɱ me sutaɱ:|| ||

Ekaɱ samayaɱ Bhagavā Sāvatthiyaɱ viharati.|| ||

Tatra kho Bhagavā bhikkhū āmantesi:|| ||

"Bhikkhavo" ti.|| ||

"Bhadante" ti te bhikkhū Bhagavato paccassosuɱ.|| ||

Bhagavā etad avoca:|| ||

 

 

Rāgassa

Abhiññāya

Rāgassa bhikkhave abhiññāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kāye kāy'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Vedanāsu vedan'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Citte citt'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Dhammesu Dhamm'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Rāgassa bhikkhave abhiññāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbāti.|| ||

■

Rāgassa bhikkhave abhiññāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu anuppannānaɱ pāpakānaɱ akusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ anuppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Uppannānaɱ pāpakānaɱ akusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ pahāṇāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggāṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Anuppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ uppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhīyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Rāgassa bhikkhave abhiññāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā ti.|| ||

■

Rāgassa bhikkhave abhiññāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu chanda-samādhi-padhāna-saŋakhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Viriya-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Citta-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Vīmaɱsa-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Rāgassa bhikkhave abhiññāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbāti.|| ||

 

§

Pariññāya

Rāgassa bhikkhave pariññāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kāye kāy'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Vedanāsu vedan'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Citte citt'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Dhammesu Dhamm'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Rāgassa bhikkhave pariññāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbāti.|| ||

■

Rāgassa bhikkhave pariññāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu anuppannānaɱ pāpakānaɱ akusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ anuppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Uppannānaɱ pāpakānaɱ akusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ pahāṇāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggāṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Anuppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ uppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhīyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Rāgassa bhikkhave pariññāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā ti.|| ||

■

Rāgassa bhikkhave pariññāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu chanda-samādhi-padhāna-saŋakhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Viriya-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Citta-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Vīmaɱsa-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Rāgassa bhikkhave pariññāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbāti.|| ||

ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Vīmaɱsa-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Rāgassa bhikkhave parikkhayāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbāti.|| ||

§

Vayāya

ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

§

Nirodhāya

Anuppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ uppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhīyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Mohassa bhikkhave khayāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā ti.|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhīyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Paḷāsassa bhikkhave vayāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā ti.|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu chanda-samādhi-padhāna-saŋakhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Viriya-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Vīmaɱsa-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Issāya bhikkhave pahānāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbāti.|| ||

Thambhassa bhikkhave khayāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā ti.|| ||

Pamādassa bhikkhave khayāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu kāye kāy'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Vedanāsu vedan'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Citte citt'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Dhammesu Dhamm'ānupassī viharati||
ātāpī sampajāno satimā vineyya loke abhijjhā-domanassaɱ.|| ||

Pamādassa bhikkhave khayāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbāti.|| ||

■

Pamādassa bhikkhave khayāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā.|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu anuppannānaɱ pāpakānaɱ akusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ anuppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Uppannānaɱ pāpakānaɱ akusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ pahāṇāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggāṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Anuppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ uppādāya chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Uppannānaɱ kusalānaɱ dhammānaɱ ṭhitiyā asammosāya bhīyobhāvāya vepullāya bhāvanāya pāripūriyā chandaɱ janeti vāyamati viriyaɱ ārabhati cittaɱ paggaṇhāti padahati.|| ||

Pamādassa bhikkhave khayāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā ti.|| ||

■

Pamādassa bhikkhave khayāya cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbā|| ||

Katame cattāro?|| ||

Idha, bhikkhave, bhikkhu chanda-samādhi-padhāna-saŋakhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Viriya-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Citta-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Vīmaɱsa-samādhi-padhāna-sankhāra-samannāgataɱ iddhi-pādaɱ bhāveti.|| ||

Pamādassa bhikkhave khayāya ime cattāro dhammā bhāvetabbāti.|| ||
